(* Additional processing to handle clocks - in CODESYS, it only starts
    with rising edge and can not be placed inside IF statement *) 
IF(tup0) THEN
    treset0 := TRUE;
ELSIF(tstart0 AND (NOT tup0)) THEN
    tup0 := TRUE;  treset0 := FALSE;
END_IF;
IF(treset0) THEN
	IF(count0=TVALUE0) THEN
		q_0 := TRUE; (*第二个周期赋值成功*)
		
	ELSE
		(*count0 := count0 + 1;	 *)
		count0 := TVALUE0;
	END_IF;
ELSE
	q_0 := FALSE;	
	count0 := 0;
END_IF;
